info:Stayed in September 2023

posted:Posted October 1, 2023
msg:I am usually busy, and it is rare that I have an 8-day holiday during the National Day, so I took my family out to relax. I compared many hotels online and finally chose Lingli Muli. The first time I came here, I knew that my choice was not wrong.
Lingli Muli is in an excellent location, just opposite the Metasequoia King Park. Living here, it is very convenient to go to any scenic spot in Guling.
The large lawn in Lingli Muli allows babies to run all day, and there are slides and swimming pools, so the babies have a lot of fun!
The two young ladies at the front desk were very enthusiastic. When they learned that we had two elderly people to take care of, they took the initiative to move our rooms together. Thank you!
When we arrived, it was more than eleven o'clock in the afternoon. We were very tired and didn't want to go out for food. We thought about eating something in the hotel restaurant. Unexpectedly, the taste surprised us very much, not inferior to some big hotels in the city, especially the pickled fish, which was tender and large, and super value!
I will choose Lingli Muli for my next vacation!
